puṇyaśloko manasi satataṃ sannidhiṃ me prayātu ityatra vākye prastutortho yathāsau puṇyaślokaḥ parameśvaro me manasi satataṃ sannidhiṃ prayātu yasya vigrahe śarīre laṅkṛtīnāṃ kaustubhabhūṣaṇaānāṃ dyutibhiradhikam aujjvalyaṃyatpādānte laghurnikṛṣṭo pi patan gauravaṃ gurutvam uttamatvaṃ samprayāti asau puṇyaślokaḥ kīdṛśaḥ chandasi vede siddhākṣararūpā askhalanarūpā tanuryasya tādṛśaḥ sadruṇa aiśvaryyarūpaguṇavān śabdamūrttidharasyaite viṣṇoraṃśā iti viṣṇupurāṇam atra śliṣṭaviśeṣaṇairvyañjanayā puṇyasyottamaślokasya kaviriva pratītiḥ  tasyāpi vigrahe samāse laṅkṛtīnām anuprāsopamādīnāṃ dyutibhiḥ śobhābhiradhikam aujjvalyaṃ tatpādasya caturthabhāgasyānte patato laghuvarṇasyāpi padāntago gururveti chandaḥśāstre uktatvāt asau chandasānuṣṭubtvādicchandasā siddho varṇamayamūrttiḥ
